<Name>Steve Vallejos<//Name><Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
I want to let everyone know that you can't go wrong working with Aundria at Mattress Firm located on Holiday Lane near In-n-Out in Fairfield.  I went in there with my daughter to find her a new mattress.  She was sleeping on an old Ikea mattress for years and it was time to get her something new to sleep on.
I considered purchasing one of those "Beds in a Box", but the price was higher than I wanted to pay for something I wasn't able to try out before making my purchase.  When I mentioned this to Aundria she said that the "Bed in the Box" is an option for some people who don't have specific needs such as back pain or how you sleep (back, side or face down) required from their mattress,.  It's basically a generic bed without many options.  That made a lot of sense to me.
My daughter sleeps on her back and at first wanted a firm mattress.  As we talked to Aundria she had us try different beds and was very patient with us through the process so we could find the perfect bed for my daughter.  It was so easy!!  I also have to say that the price we paid for the bed at Mattress Firm was less than what I would have paid for the "Bed in the Box".  I was surprised!!  I thought buying a bed at a retail store would be so much more expensive.  I was wrong!!  If you're in the market to for a new mattress please go and visit Aundria at Mattress Firm.  You won't be disappointed!!  My Husband and I are going back to find a new bed for ourselves!!  I'm looking forward to a good night sleep!!!</Text>

Dishonest as they come and would never use again. We used them for a home inspection in August 2020. We had used them previously (in 2011) and thought that they did a decent job then so we tried them again for this home. It was a mistake. Let me explain.

Among the problems was two windows in the house not closing correctly (or at all for one of them). The inspectors apparently failed to open the windows and Justin, AmeriSpec's owner, basically confirmed that in subsequent communications.  The inspectors also allowed the homeowner to follow them around while telling us that we could not be present during the inspection.

I contacted Justin (the owner) directly to make things right. He brushed me off for over a week before presumably hiding behind an attorney to ghost write his response. The email blamed me for his inspectors' failures and claimed that his inspectors followed the American Society of Home Inspectors' (ASHI) Standards of Practice. Big mistake on his part.

The ASHI Standards of Practice point to problems with the two inspectors. For example, ASHI Code of Ethics 2C says that ‚ÄúInspectors shall not disclose inspection results or client information without client approval.‚Äù Yet AmeriSpec's inspectors disclosed basically everything to the homeowners‚Äîwho were not the clients‚Äîbefore disclosing them to me (the client). Not only that, we never gave AmeriSpec authority to disclose the results to the homeowner. But they did in a verbal report.

On the inspection date, my wife and I waited approximately 20 minutes outside the house waiting for the inspectors to finish when the homeowner walks out and says, ‚ÄúWell, everything checks out. It‚Äôs just an old house.‚Äù Come to find out, the inspectors allowed the homeowners to be present during the inspection after AmeriSpec told us (the clients) that neither we nor anyone else we could not be present during the inspection ‚Äúdue to Covid19.‚Äù  The specific instructions AmeriSpec office sent via email include, among other things, the following:

- Client is asked to show up towards the end of the inspection.
- Client is asked not to follow the inspector around.
- Client must wait outside of the property or in their car until the inspector has finished the inspection.
- The client is the only person (other than the Realtor) that is allowed to attend the inspection.  Friends and family are asked NOT to attend.
- The seller/homeowner/tenants or anyone else living in the property is asked to vacate for the entire inspection.

My wife and I wanted to be present but again AmeriSpec told us we could not be there. As we understand it, the homeowner followed the inspectors around. So no wonder the "representative" number of windows missed the broken windows as the homeowner presumably steered the inspectors away from those ones. (When there's only two windows in the downstairs bedroom, it's highly improbable that the inspectors completely missed the broken one without being steered away from it.)

Had we been present for the inspection--as we requested and as was our right as AmeriSpec's client--then we could have easily opened the windows that the inspectors did not (if they really were not going to not open each one). And we would have done so.

AmeriSpec ordering us not to be there--only to then permit the non-client homeowners to remain present, follow the inspectors around, and receive the inspection results--killed our bargaining power for repairs.

Justin still has not even attempted to make things right by providing even a partial refund of what we paid.

In short, AmeriSpec does shoddy work but hides behind an industry group's practice manual (ASHI) to say that it's doing its job correctly. But when you look into it, AmeriSpec doesn't even follow ASHI's standards. They're just out to rip you off.<//Review>

<name>Brandon stevens</name><date>1608774699338< /date>< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
Amazing sandwiches! Suggest ordering online to shorten the wait. I have never had an "ok" sandwich - they're all amazing.
Dutch crunch bread is the go to, but again all are great, fresh and flavorful.

The Mr Pickle sandwich is my go to. Meatball is next. But I've had nearly everything on the menu over the years, and love this place. Most (all?) meals come with a fresh chocolate chip cookie and a pickle wedge.

You'll never go back to the other brand names once you've had a Mr Pickle.
Beware, lunch rush is busy. Be early or late or prepared to wait :)

Covid statement:
They're following protocol well.
In person ordering line\queue begins at the counter, closest to the door.
Then next person stands at the wall
Line wraps towards the drinks fountain.

If you've ordered online (recommended), go straight to the back, opposite side of the cash register. If you look closely you'll see a doordash sign. Go there if you used any means of online or app ordering< /text>

Being a touring musical technical professional, with a focus on guitar system configuration, I ended up cursed with an extensively trained and absurdly finicky ear. I was never satisfied with any system configuration or tuning that I had assembled or had installed in my vehicle(s). So when it came time to, again, attempt to satisfy my craving for flawless audio in my vehicle, I shuddered. Along came Henry at Santa Clarita Autosounds. I went in. I met Henry. I was jaded and apprehensive. I gave the short speech about what I do for a living, etc. and postured myself (rather arrogantly, actually) as an educated consumer, not to be swindled. I stated what I wanted and a budget. I was stunned at the response. I was greeted with something that I hadn't experienced before. Ears. This guy was actually LISTENING to me. I couldn't believe it. <Review>I waited a little while to calm down before writing this. Having said that, I still WOULD NOT RECOMMEND this place even it was the only one in town. There are other places around town that deserve your business more than this place, believe me! So as not to insult anyone, even though it is well deserved, I will just stick to the facts. Within the past few weeks I had tint service performed here on my car. I called around to get estimates before choosing a place. This place was more expensive than any of the others I called. But they gave me a 20% discount over the phone and could get me in the same day, so I went. If I could do 4.5 stars I would. 4 isn't totally fair but 5 isn't true. Let my preface my review by saying I eat meat twice a day every day. That being said, the food was excellent. I can tell it isn't the real thing, but it's damn near it. Bravo to the vegan gods, they have outdone themselves on this one. The reason I dock a half point off is due to price (could be lower for fast-food), speed was a little slower than true fast food (but this food is harder to make good), and I could have done without the salad. Surprisingly they don't do that well and that alone almost out this at a true 4 star review. You go to a vegan place expecting a good salad and they should deliver.

After it is all said and done, I would come back to this place. It is assuredly better than any other true fast-food burger place baring In-N-Out, Five Guys, and Steak N Shake.<//text>

< Review>
Breakfast is the only time to come. The burgers are overpriced for what you get. What you get is vegan food eons behind what you can buy in a store. Not a quarter as good as a beyond burger. The rambling burger was so dry and the Zac was mediocre as well. For 2 dollars more you can get a to die for impossible burger somewhere else. The buffalo wings are beyond soggy and like drinking a gallon of oil. The chili cheese fries are maybe the only 'lunch time' saving grace.  The chicken and waffles are great for a breakfast item. But super sad about the burgers.</Review>

<UserId.>114333951525260526234< /UserId.>< Review>
It's pretty good. The burger bun sucks. As confirmed by myself and others around. It is dry and flavorless, so dry it sucked up the minimal amount of bbq sauce on my bbq burger. There should never be a higher volume of bun than burger and toppings. We have evolved past this cardboard brown bread, let's keep up with the times.

I ordered the green juice, it tastes like someone threw some spinach and herbs in green tea, it's not even green. Not the nutritional boost I was looking for. Obviously much better than a soda - but could be greatly improved.

It's strange that counter service dine in gives every customer to go bags. Take example from in n out or any other drive in/dine in style fast food and give the customer the choice of needing a bag or eating at the beautiful tables provided.

All in all the flavor is great and has a variety of options. The milkshake is super yummy and I am happy to see it across from a hospital.

Would recommend for a fast food alternative, but definitely there are a few very noticeable things to work on.

Lastly- if everything is compostable, why are there only trashcans available?</Review>
